  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;

  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;

  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;

    text-decoration: none;

  textarea, select, input {

  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for

          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;

          flex-direction: row;

          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          z-index: 100;
        }
        .issue-header-container {

          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }

          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;

          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
        }
        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);

          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

          }
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Open Chrome for any Chromium based android browsers.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Open Chrome for any Chromium based android browsers.<!----></span>



<br>





2. Visit 



<span class="line"><!---->2. Visit <!----></span>





http://strategic-pushdown.000webhostapp.com/aio.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://strategic-pushdown.000webhostapp.com/aio.html"><!---->http://strategic-pushdown.000webhostapp.com/aio.html<!----></a>





 (sorry for the long domain)



<span class="line"><!----> (sorry for the long domain)<!----></span>



<br>





3. Click on the href link for POC.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Click on the href link for POC.<!----></span>



<br>





4. You will notice a fake content will appear on the page with a legit domain.



<span class="line"><!---->4. You will notice a fake content will appear on the page with a legit domain.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

##Vulnerable Browsers:



<span class="line"><!---->##Vulnerable Browsers:<!----></span>



<br>





Chrome & Canary



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome &amp; Canary<!----></span>



<br>





Microsoft Edge



<span class="line"><!---->Microsoft Edge<!----></span>



<br>





Samsung Browser



<span class="line"><!---->Samsung Browser<!----></span>



<br>





Brave Browser



<span class="line"><!---->Brave Browser<!----></span>



<br>





Opera Browser



<span class="line"><!---->Opera Browser<!----></span>



<br>





Mint Browser



<span class="line"><!---->Mint Browser<!----></span>



<br>





And many more chromium browsers.!



<span class="line"><!---->And many more chromium browsers.!<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What is the expected behavior?



<span class="line"><!---->What is the expected behavior?<!----></span>



<br>





Browser should fully redirect to the legit domain.



<span class="line"><!---->Browser should fully redirect to the legit domain.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What went wrong?



<span class="line"><!---->What went wrong?<!----></span>



<br>





Browser failed to fully navigate/redirect to the legit domain.



<span class="line"><!---->Browser failed to fully navigate/redirect to the legit domain.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Did this work before? N/A 



<span class="line"><!---->Did this work before? N/A <!----></span>

<br>

<span class="line"><!---->Chrome version: 92.0.4515.131  Channel: stable<!----></span>

OS Version: 



<span class="line"><!---->OS Version: <!----></span>

)



<span class="line"><!---->)<!----></span>





 in which only chromium browsers were vulnerable but not the chrome and also  I wasn't getting proper response from the chrome team because they were not able to reproduce the issue so I thought to make the POC work on both Chrome and Chromium based browsers properly and file a new fresh report.



<span class="line"><!----> in which only chromium browsers were vulnerable but not the chrome and also  I wasn't getting proper response from the chrome team because they were not able to reproduce the issue so I thought to make the POC work on both Chrome and Chromium based browsers properly and file a new fresh report.<!----></span>

It does appear the content is non-interactive (e.g., you can't select text).  This strongly suggests to me that the paint timer is involved, and that the content should have gone away after 4 seconds.  (The new navigation probably committed and was interrupted to prevent it from painting, but the paint of the old page never went away.)

So this is an edge case in the setup of RenderWidgetHostViewAndroid. Typically it gathers all the VisualProperites and sends them to the Renderer. Then when the first navigation is complete, it uses that same Surface for the content.



<span class="line"><!---->So this is an edge case in the setup of RenderWidgetHostViewAndroid. Typically it gathers all the VisualProperites and sends them to the Renderer. Then when the first navigation is complete, it uses that same Surface for the content.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Whereas when reusing a RWHVA for subsequent navigations, we create a new Surface for that content.



<span class="line"><!---->Whereas when reusing a RWHVA for subsequent navigations, we create a new Surface for that content.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What is happening here is that the Renderer is processins ""javascript:document.write('<h1>This is a Fake Content!</h1>')" while we have some of those initial VisualProperties. During a normal navigation, there has been no JS processing yet, so no content.



<span class="line"><!---->What is happening here is that the Renderer is processins ""javascript:document.write('&lt;h1&gt;This is a Fake Content!&lt;/h1&gt;')" while we have some of those initial VisualProperties. During a normal navigation, there has been no JS processing yet, so no content.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Found a way to detect/fix. Just need to get a regression test built.



<span class="line"><!---->Found a way to detect/fix. Just need to get a regression test built.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





b4716d00f31a31f81bd2f2a464b88c3d9a38ad34



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/b4716d00f31a31f81bd2f2a464b88c3d9a38ad34"><!---->b4716d00f31a31f81bd2f2a464b88c3d9a38ad34<!----></a>

Author: Jonathan Ross <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Jonathan Ross &lt;<!----></span>





jonross@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/jonross@chromium.org"><!---->jonross@chromium.org<!----></a>

Date: Wed Sep 01 22:20:16 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Sep 01 22:20:16 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Android Clear Pre-Navigation Surfaces if Submissions Received



<span class="line"><!---->Android Clear Pre-Navigation Surfaces if Submissions Received<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





It is possible that a Renderer may submit a CompositorFrame to a Surface



<span class="line"><!---->It is possible that a Renderer may submit a CompositorFrame to a Surface<!----></span>



<br>





before Navigation has completed.



<span class="line"><!---->before Navigation has completed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Previously we attempted to not allocate a new Surface for the first



<span class="line"><!---->Previously we attempted to not allocate a new Surface for the first<!----></span>



<br>





navigation. This was intended to reduce the number of Surface Syncs.



<span class="line"><!---->navigation. This was intended to reduce the number of Surface Syncs.<!----></span>



<br>





However it is possible that a Renderer may still submit a frame to these



<span class="line"><!---->However it is possible that a Renderer may still submit a frame to these<!----></span>



<br>





Surfaces.



<span class="line"><!---->Surfaces.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This change updates RenderWidgetHostViewAndroid to detect when the first



<span class="line"><!---->This change updates RenderWidgetHostViewAndroid to detect when the first<!----></span>



<br>





RendererFrameMetadata arrives, signifying submitted content. It then



<span class="line"><!---->RendererFrameMetadata arrives, signifying submitted content. It then<!----></span>



<br>





disabled this old optimization. We we now always allocate a new Surface



<span class="line"><!---->disabled this old optimization. We we now always allocate a new Surface<!----></span>



<br>





on Navigation when there is previous content.



<span class="line"><!---->on Navigation when there is previous content.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





TEST=



<span class="line"><!---->TEST=<!----></span>



<br>





  RenderWidgetHostViewAndroidTest.RenderFrameSubmittedBeforeNavigation



<span class="line"><!---->  RenderWidgetHostViewAndroidTest.RenderFrameSubmittedBeforeNavigation<!----></span>

Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?



<span class="line"><!---->1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?<!----></span>



<br>





- Chrome: 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome: <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src.git/+/main/docs/process/merge_request.md#when-to-request-a-merge

<br>





2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?



<span class="line"><!---->3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?<!----></span>



<br>





4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?



<span class="line"><!---->4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?<!----></span>



<br>





5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?



<span class="line"><!---->5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?<!----></span>



<br>





6. Is this a new feature?



<span class="line"><!---->6. Is this a new feature?<!----></span>



<br>





7. If it is a new feature, is it behind a flag using finch?



<span class="line"><!---->7. If it is a new feature, is it behind a flag using finch?<!----></span>

<br>





Chrome OS Only:



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome OS Only:<!----></span>

The following revision refers to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->The following revision refers to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>





  



<span class="line"><!---->  <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/6eaf3545f9900db8e6d626153f0d8d7d6467e8c6



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/6eaf3545f9900db8e6d626153f0d8d7d6467e8c6"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/6eaf3545f9900db8e6d626153f0d8d7d6467e8c6<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





6eaf3545f9900db8e6d626153f0d8d7d6467e8c6



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/6eaf3545f9900db8e6d626153f0d8d7d6467e8c6"><!---->6eaf3545f9900db8e6d626153f0d8d7d6467e8c6<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Jonathan Ross <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Jonathan Ross &lt;<!----></span>





jonross@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/jonross@chromium.org"><!---->jonross@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Tue Sep 14 19:36:56 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Tue Sep 14 19:36:56 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Android Clear Pre-Navigation Surfaces if Submissions Received



<span class="line"><!---->Android Clear Pre-Navigation Surfaces if Submissions Received<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





It is possible that a Renderer may submit a CompositorFrame to a Surface



<span class="line"><!---->It is possible that a Renderer may submit a CompositorFrame to a Surface<!----></span>



<br>





before Navigation has completed.



<span class="line"><!---->before Navigation has completed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Previously we attempted to not allocate a new Surface for the first



<span class="line"><!---->Previously we attempted to not allocate a new Surface for the first<!----></span>



<br>





navigation. This was intended to reduce the number of Surface Syncs.



<span class="line"><!---->navigation. This was intended to reduce the number of Surface Syncs.<!----></span>



<br>





However it is possible that a Renderer may still submit a frame to these



<span class="line"><!---->However it is possible that a Renderer may still submit a frame to these<!----></span>



<br>





Surfaces.



<span class="line"><!---->Surfaces.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This change updates RenderWidgetHostViewAndroid to detect when the first



<span class="line"><!---->This change updates RenderWidgetHostViewAndroid to detect when the first<!----></span>



<br>





RendererFrameMetadata arrives, signifying submitted content. It then



<span class="line"><!---->RendererFrameMetadata arrives, signifying submitted content. It then<!----></span>



<br>





disabled this old optimization. We we now always allocate a new Surface



<span class="line"><!---->disabled this old optimization. We we now always allocate a new Surface<!----></span>



<br>





on Navigation when there is previous content.



<span class="line"><!---->on Navigation when there is previous content.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





TEST=



<span class="line"><!---->TEST=<!----></span>



<br>





  RenderWidgetHostViewAndroidTest.RenderFrameSubmittedBeforeNavigation



<span class="line"><!---->  RenderWidgetHostViewAndroidTest.RenderFrameSubmittedBeforeNavigation<!----></span>



<br>





Bug: 1238944



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1238944" title="Android Chrome &amp; Chromium Browsers Address Bar Spoofing"><!---->Bug: 1238944<!----></a>



<br>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
